# CLONING LIMINE BOOTLOADER
# git clone https://github.com/limine-bootloader/limine.git --branch=v8.x-binary --depth=1
# make -C limine
# Creating build directory which will be used to create ISO image, kernel.bin and object files
mkdir -p build
# Creating ISO directory which will be used to create ISO image 
mkdir -p iso_root/boot
# Copying files to ISO directory and creating directories 
cp src/img/boot_loader_wallpaper.bmp  iso_root/boot/boot_loader_wallpaper.bmp
cp -v build/kernel.bin iso_root/boot/
'build/kernel.bin' -> 'iso_root/boot/kernel.bin'
mkdir -p iso_root/boot/limine
cp -v src/limine.conf src/limine/limine-bios.sys src/limine/limine-bios-cd.bin src/limine/limine-uefi-cd.bin iso_root/boot/limine/
'src/limine.conf' -> 'iso_root/boot/limine/limine.conf'
'src/limine/limine-bios.sys' -> 'iso_root/boot/limine/limine-bios.sys'
'src/limine/limine-bios-cd.bin' -> 'iso_root/boot/limine/limine-bios-cd.bin'
'src/limine/limine-uefi-cd.bin' -> 'iso_root/boot/limine/limine-uefi-cd.bin'
mkdir -p iso_root/EFI/BOOT
cp -v src/limine/BOOTX64.EFI iso_root/EFI/BOOT/
'src/limine/BOOTX64.EFI' -> 'iso_root/EFI/BOOT/BOOTX64.EFI'
cp -v src/limine/BOOTIA32.EFI iso_root/EFI/BOOT/
'src/limine/BOOTIA32.EFI' -> 'iso_root/EFI/BOOT/BOOTIA32.EFI'
# Creating initrd.cpio module for bootloader. These files can be used for various purposes,
cp -v src/initrd/initrd.cpio iso_root/boot/initrd.cpio
'src/initrd/initrd.cpio' -> 'iso_root/boot/initrd.cpio'
# Creating KeblaOS-0.11-image.iso file by using xorriso.
xorriso -as mkisofs -b boot/limine/limine-bios-cd.bin -no-emul-boot -boot-load-size 4 -boot-info-table --efi-boot boot/limine/limine-uefi-cd.bin -efi-boot-part --efi-boot-image --protective-msdos-label iso_root -o build/KeblaOS-0.12-image.iso
src/limine/limine bios-install build/KeblaOS-0.12-image.iso
# automatically clean up all object files from build directory.
make clean
make[1]: Entering directory '/mnt/b/Git-Projects/GitHub/baponkar/KeblaOS'
rm -f build/*.o
#rm -rf iso_root
make[1]: Leaving directory '/mnt/b/Git-Projects/GitHub/baponkar/KeblaOS'
make run
make[1]: Entering directory '/mnt/b/Git-Projects/GitHub/baponkar/KeblaOS'
# GDB Debuging
# qemu-system-x86_64 -cdrom build/KeblaOS-0.12-image.iso -m 4096 -serial file:debug/serial_output.log -d guest_errors,int,cpu_reset -D debug/qemu.log -vga std -machine q35 -smp cores=2,threads=2,sockets=1,maxcpus=4 -s -S -rtc base=utc,clock=host
# UEFI Boot
# qemu-system-x86_64 -hda build/disk.img -cdrom build/KeblaOS-0.12-image.iso -m 4096 -serial file:debug/serial_output.log -d guest_errors,int,cpu_reset -D debug/qemu.log -vga std -machine q35 -smp cores=2,threads=2,sockets=1,maxcpus=4 -bios /usr/share/OVMF/OVMF_CODE.fd  -rtc base=utc,clock=host
# BIOS Boot
qemu-system-x86_64 \
	-machine q35 \
	-m 4096 \
	-smp cores=4,threads=1,sockets=1,maxcpus=4 \
	-hda build/disk.img \
	-cdrom build/KeblaOS-0.12-image.iso \
	-serial stdio \
	-d guest_errors,int,cpu_reset \
	-D debug/qemu.log \
	-vga std
